[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"1-byte-write-heap-buffer-overflow-far-from-bounds"[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The write operation attempts to access a [0m[32m"wild pointer"[0m[39m that is outside the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid heap allocation range[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack Analysis:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The error originates from the following execution path:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This leads to `freerdp_certificate_data_new_nocopy`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Which calls `freerdp_certificate_data_load_cache`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Then `freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Finally reaching the problematic function `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m in `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory State:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The shadow bytes around the buggy address show all bytes marked as `fa` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleft redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating the accessed memory is in a heap redzone area[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The accessed address `[0m[1;36m0x502000010230[0m[39m` falls within a region that should not be[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwritten to, suggesting either an off-by-one error or incorrect bounds checking[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Affected Components:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The vulnerability is triggered through the certificate handling subsystem, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically when processing PEM-formatted certificate data. The affected files and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions include:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate.c[0m[39m` - Contains the vulnerable [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/crypto/[0m[95mcertificate_data.c[0m[39m` - Contains the certificate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata loading and caching logic[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Areas Requiring Investigation:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this issue, the following components [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Location:** The `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` function in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`certificate.c` at line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m, particularly the buffer write operation that causes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe overflow[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Data Flow:** The certificate data loading path from [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem` through [0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation:** Buffer allocation and size calculations in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex` to determine if the allocated buffer size is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient for the data being written[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Input Validation:** PEM parsing logic to identify if there are missing bounds [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks or incorrect size calculations when processing malformed or edge-case PEM [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Related Functions:** Any other functions in the certificate handling subsystem[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability can potentially be triggered by specially crafted PEM certificate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata, as demonstrated by the fuzzer test case located at `[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`.[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m148[0m[39m:rdpCertificateData* [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_data_new_from_pem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char* hostname,[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m155[0m[39m:    [0m[39mrdpCertificateData* data = [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_data_new_nocopy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhostname, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mport, cert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m156[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!data[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m157[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibfreerdp/crypto/certificate.[0m[1;92mc:1397[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1400[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1397[0m[39m:rdpCertificate* [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_new_from_pem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char* pem[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1398[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1399[0m[39m:   [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;35mfreerdp_certificate_new_from[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpem, FALSE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1400[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe heap-buffer-overflow occurs in `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` at line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `libfreerdp/crypto/certificate.c`. The function has three critical bugs:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Integer Overflow**: Uses `uint16_t` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-bit, max [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m535[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for `blocksize`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`offset`, and `length` variables, which causes integer wraparound when processing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPEM data larger than ~65KB[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Missing Bounds Check**: Loop condition `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` doesn't verify [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat `offset < length`, allowing `offset` to exceed buffer boundaries[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Missing Early Termination**: No check after reading to stop when the buffer is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlike the correct implementation in `bio_read_pem`[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered when:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A certificate contains the policy OID [0m[32m"2.23.140.1.2.1"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchecked at line [0m[1;36m1633[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buggy `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` is called instead of the safe [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`bio_read_pem`[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Large PEM data causes `uint16_t` overflow, resulting in incorrect buffer size [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculations[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The null terminator write at line [0m[1;36m1570[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m occurs at an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds location[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Approach: Align `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` with the Correct [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImplementation**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe safest fix is to make `freerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy` functionally identical[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto `bio_read_pem` in terms of buffer management, since the policy check should not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect how PEM data is read from a BIO.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step-by-step implementation from the initial codebase:**[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fix variable types** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1537[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1539[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `const uint16_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;` to `const size_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `uint16_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;` to `size_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `uint16_t length = blocksize;` to `size_t length = blocksize;`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: `size_t` is the proper type for memory sizes and prevents [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteger overflow on [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit systems[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fix loop condition** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1546[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: This ensures the loop terminates when `offset` reaches [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`length`, preventing out-of-bounds access even if `BIO_read` keeps returning data[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Add early termination check** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1566[0m[39m, before line [0m[1;36m1567[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After `offset += [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mstatus;`, add:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         break;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: This stops the loop immediately when there's still space in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer but we've finished reading [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents unnecessary reallocation and potential [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missues[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Update status variable declaration** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1532[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `int status = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;` to `const int status` inside the loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmove [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclaration to line [0m[1;36m1556[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Or keep as is but ensure proper scoping[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Rationale**: The variable should be const where possible to match the safe [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation pattern[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The corrected function should match this structure:**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic BOOL [0m[1;35mfreerdp_bio_read_pem_with_policy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBIO* bio, char** ppem, size_t* [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplength[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    BOOL rc = FALSE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mWINPR_ASSERT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mWINPR_ASSERT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mppem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    const size_t blocksize = [0m[1;36m2048[0m[39m;      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from uint16_t[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    size_t offset = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;                  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from uint16_t[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    size_t length = blocksize;          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from uint16_t[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    char* pem = NULL;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *ppem = NULL;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mplength[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *plength = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    while [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset < length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Changed from: while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        char* tmp = [0m[1;35mrealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpem, length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!tmp[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            goto fail;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        pem = tmp;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mERR_clear_error[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        const int status = [0m[1;35mBIO_read[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"failed to read certificate"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            goto fail;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstatus == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            break;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        offset += [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mstatus;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ADDED: early termination check[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            break;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        length += blocksize;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    pem[0m[1;39m[[0m[39moffset[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;                [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Now safe: offset <= length, buffer size =[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength + [0m[1;36m1[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    *ppem = pem;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mplength[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        *plength = offset;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    rc = TRUE;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!rc[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return rc;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The policy check at line [0m[1;36m1633[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function signature and return behavior are identical[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The RFC [0m[1;36m7299[0m[39m policy handling intent is preserved[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`freerdp_certificate_get_pem_ex`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work without [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses All Issues:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Integer overflow**: Using `size_t` prevents wraparound for large certificates [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcan handle multi-GB data if needed[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Missing bounds check**: Loop condition `offset < length` ensures we never [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed buffer bounds[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Missing early termination**: The `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength - offset > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break;` check [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents unnecessary iterations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Matches Proven Safe Implementation:**[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix exactly mirrors the working `bio_read_pem` function[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This function has been used successfully in the codebase without issues[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reduces maintenance burden by having consistent implementations[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests will pass as the function behavior is identical, just safer[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer test will no longer trigger the overflow[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Certificate handling for both policy and non-policy certificates works correctly[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effects:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m expected**: The change only affects internal buffer management, not the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI or functionality[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function will now correctly handle large certificates [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>65KB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that previously[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwould have failed[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Testing**: The existing fuzzer test will verify the fix[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Regression testing**: All certificate-related tests should be run to ensure no [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality breaks[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Memory usage**: The change to `size_t` slightly increases stack memory usage [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes per variable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but this is negligible[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `bio_read_pem` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1477[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1527[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the exact same pattern[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand has been working correctly[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is a proven approach already present in the codebase[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Alternative Approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNot Recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn alternative would be to simply remove the policy-specific function and always [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse `bio_read_pem`:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m At line [0m[1;36m1633[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1637[0m[39m, change to:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mbio_read_pem[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbio, &pem, pLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why not recommended:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The policy check suggests there was intent to add policy-specific handling[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing the function entirely might break future requirements[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Better to fix the implementation than remove functionality[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the fix:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Run the fuzzer test: `TestFuzzCryptoCertificateDataSetPEM -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Verify no ASan errors occur[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Check that certificate data is correctly parsed from PEM[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensure both policy and non-policy certificates work correctly[0m                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
